============================================================
GT Equivalence Verification (BPG4)
============================================================
GT: c0*(c1 - P/c2)*P + c3*P/(c4 + exp(-c5*(-c6 + P)))
Candidate formulas: 50

Let  
\[
\text{GT}(P)=0.1727856699554779\,(1-P/48.5483027446097)\,P\;+\;0.1727856699554779\;\frac{P}{1+\exp\!\big(-1.5237423595759925\,(P-0.9236923548638324)\big)}.
\]
Key structural facts about GT:

- **No \(t\)-dependence at all**. Any candidate with unavoidable \(t\) dependence must be killed by setting coefficients to 0.
- GT is the sum of:
  1) a **quadratic polynomial in \(P\)**: \(aP - bP^2\) with \(a=0.1727856...\), \(b=0.1727856.../48.5483...\neq 0\);
  2) a **logistic term**: \(k \, P/(1+\exp(-m(P-p_0)))\) with \(k,m,p_0\neq 0\).
- Therefore any matching candidate must be able to represent **(quadratic in \(P\)) + (logistic-in-\(P\) term)**. None of the candidates contain an \(\exp(\text{affine in }P)\) in a denominator of the form \(1+\exp(\cdot)\). So the only way a candidate could match is if it can *somehow* reproduce that logistic term via other primitives (sin, cos, tanh, rational powers, logs, etc.). That is impossible as an identity for all real \(P\) because the logistic term is not a rational function, not a finite combination of algebraic terms, and not representable by the specific non-exponential forms present (and candidates that do have \(\tanh\) still lack the required \(P\)-dependent \(\tanh\) structure; they have \(\tanh(\text{affine in }t)\), not \(\tanh(\text{affine in }P)\)).

Below I go candidate by candidate, focusing on whether (i) all \(t\)-dependence can be removed, and (ii) the remaining \(P\)-dependence can equal “quadratic + logistic”.

---

### Candidate 1
\(P^2c0 + Pc1 + P^{c2}c3\sin(c4 t+c5)+ \frac{c6}{(P^2c7+1)^5}+ \frac{c8}{P^2}\)

- Can remove \(t\)-term by setting \(c3=0\).
- Remaining terms are polynomial \(P^2, P\) plus rational-in-\(P\) pieces \((P^2c7+1)^{-5}\) and \(1/P^2\).
- No way to produce the logistic \(P/(1+\exp(\alpha P+\beta))\) term. **No match**.

### Candidate 2
\(P^2c0 + Pc1 + P + c2 + c3/t^2 + \frac{c4}{(P^2c5+1)^5} + c6\log(c7 t+1)\cos(Pc8)/P^3\)

- Must eliminate \(t\): set \(c3=0\) and \(c6=0\).
- Left with polynomial + constant + rational \((P^2c5+1)^{-5}\).
- Still no logistic term. **No match**.

### Candidate 3
Same as 2 but with \(4P\). After killing \(t\)-terms, still polynomial/constant/rational only. **No match**.

### Candidate 4

### Candidate 46
\(P^2c0 + Pc1 + \frac{Pc2}{P+c3} + \frac{c4}{(P^2c5+1)^5} + \frac{c6}{Pc7+c3} + c8/P^2\)

No \(t\), good. But the non-polynomial parts are rational functions in \(P\). GT includes a logistic (transcendental exponential) term, not rational. Cannot match for all \(P\). **No match**.

### Candidate 47

**Conclusion:** Every candidate either (a) cannot reproduce the required logistic-in-\(P\) term at all, or (b) would need to keep \(t\)-dependent terms which GT does not have. GT: c0*(c1 - P/c2)*P + c3*P/(c4 + exp(-c5*(-c6 + P)))
Candidates evaluated: 50

I need to analyze whether any candidate can be made equivalent to the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `0.1728*(1 - P/48.55)*P + 0.1728*P/(1 + exp(-1.524*(-0.924 + P)))`

This simplifies to:
- Term 1: `0.1728*P - 0.003559*P²` (a linear + quadratic in P)
- Term 2: `0.1728*P/(1 + exp(-1.524*P + 1.408))` (a sigmoid-weighted term)

The GT is a function of **P only** (no t dependence). The key structural elements are:
1. `P²` term (quadratic)
2. `P` term (linear)
3. A sigmoid term: `P/(1 + exp(f(P)))` — this is NOT a rational function of P, it involves an exponential.

Now let me examine the candidates. Most candidates contain terms like:
- `1/(P²*c + 1)^5` — this is a rational function, NOT a sigmoid
- `log(...)`, `cos(...)`, `sin(...)`, `tanh(...)` — various basis functions
- Many have `t` dependence

**Critical observation:** The GT contains `P/(1 + exp(...))`, which is a sigmoid-type function. None of the candidates contain `exp()` in their expressions. The candidates use basis functions like:
- `1/(P²*c + 1)^5` — rational, not sigmoid
- `sin(...)`, `cos(...)`, `tanh(...)`, `log(...)`

The sigmoid function `1/(1 + exp(-aP + b))` cannot be exactly represented by any combination of polynomials, rational functions `1/(P²c+1)^5`, trigonometric functions, or logarithms. These are fundamentally different basis functions.

Let me check candidates with `tanh` (Candidates 13, 44) since `tanh` relates to sigmoid: `sigmoid(x) = (1 + tanh(x/2))/2`.

**Candidate 13:** `P²c0 + Pc1 + c2 + c3*tanh(c4*t+c5) + c6*tanh(c7*t+c8) + c9/P^5`
The tanh terms depend on `t`, not `P`. Setting coefficients to zero eliminates them, leaving `P²c0 + Pc1 + c2 + c9/P^5`, which can't match the sigmoid in P.

**Candidate 44:** `P²c0 + Pc1 + c2 + c3*tanh(c4+t) + c5*tanh(c6*t+c7) + c8/P^5`
Same issue — tanh depends on t, not P.

No candidate has a sigmoid or tanh function of **P**. The term `P/(1+exp(f(P)))` in the GT is an essential, non-trivial component that cannot be replicated by any of the basis functions present in the candidates (polynomials, `1/(P²c+1)^5`, trig functions of P or t, logs).

Let me verify: could the sigmoid term be negligible? No — per Rule 2, we need EXACT equivalence, not approximations.

For all candidates: The GT requires a sigmoid-in-P basis function that none possess.
